str_sarranid_rebellion_pretender_story_1 The_heads_of_the_Imagawa_clan_are_the_rightful_shugo_of_Suruga_province,_from_our_family_castle_in_Sunpu._Not_the_upstart,_so-called_'Tokugawa'._What_nerve--changing_their_name_from_Matsudaira_in_order_to_claim_descent_from_the_Genji!_After_we_were_beaten_by_the_Oda_clan_at_Okehazama,_the_treacherous_Matsudaira_picked_up_the_pieces.
str_swadian_rebellion_pretender_story_2 Yet_before_my_father_died,_during_his_time_of_greatest_need,_his_traitorous_vassal_Nagao_Kagetora_forced_him_to_name_him_his_heir_and_adopt_him_as_a_price_for_his_assistance_--_assistance_that_should_have_been_due_automatically_because_he_was_a_mere_vassal!.
str_vaegir_rebellion_pretender_story_2 After_my_father_was_murdered,_the_present_Lord_Date_incited_strife_among_our_hereditary_vassals_by_supporting_a_rival_claimant_as_heir._The_infighting_weakened_us_and_he_picked_up_the_pieces._As_I_think_about_it_more_and_more_during_my_exile,_I_am_now_convinced_that_Lord_Date_had_my_father_assassinated_in_the_first_place._That_is_no_way_for_a_samurai_to_act_--_a_shameful_display.
str_khergit_rebellion_pretender_story_2 I_was_still_taking_stock_of_my_province_while_Oda_turned_my_vassals._He_even_sent_me_messages_of_friendship_through_his_wife,_my_aunt._By_the_time_I_caught_wind_of_what_was_happening,_it_was_too_late._There_was_barely_even_a_battle_--_my_army_was_not_yet_close_to_ready_before_I_was_thrown_out_of_my_own_castle,_my_childhood_home.
str_nord_rebellion_pretender_story_2 My_father_was_stabbed_in_the_back_while_I_was_a_monk_in_a_temple._As_the_last_of_my_brothers_alive,_I_hurried_home_to_rally_his_armies,_but_my_ship_was_wrecked_by_a_storm._One_of_my_father's_other_vassels,_Lord_Kikkawa,_seized_this_opportunity_and_spread_rumors_that_I_had_died._Lord_Mori_then_summoned_a_gathering_of_his_supporters_to_have_himself_proclaimed_ruler,_and_has_taken_the_past_few_years_to_consolidate_his_power.
str_rhodok_rebellion_pretender_story_2 My_father_is_a_treacherous_man_that_will_surely_lead_the_Takeda_to_ruin._After_Okehazama,_he_invaded_Suruga_and_destroyed_what_remained_of_the_Imagawa_--_my_wife's_family!_They_were_allies_in_their_time_of_greatest_need,_and_my_father_destroyed_them_just_like_that.
str_sarranid_rebellion_pretender_story_2 When_the_last_Imagawa_lord_died,_it_seemed_only_natural_to_the_vassals_of_my_family_to_give_up_and_dissolve_the_clan,_so_they_could_pick_up_the_pieces_and_run_off_to_our_Oda,_Takeda,_and_Hojo_enemies.
str_swadian_rebellion_pretender_story_3 I_will_admit_that_I_did_my_cause_no_good_by_cursing_Kagetora_and_all_who_listened_to_him_as_traitors,_but_I_also_believe_that_the_hereditary_vassals_that_switched_over_were_bribed._No_matter_--_I_will_raise_an_army_of_loyal_samurai,_who_would_honor_their_old_lord's_memory_and_true_will._And_if_anyone_doubts_that_a_woman_can_wield_power,_then_I_will_take_Echigo_and_the_Kanto_by_force_to_prove_my_military_worth.
str_vaegir_rebellion_pretender_story_3 Until_I_have_my_rights_restored_in_the_sight_of_the_Date_clan,_I_will_bear_my_shame_in_exile_until_I_retake_my_birthright_by_force.
str_khergit_rebellion_pretender_story_3 Great_Lord_Oda_thinks_that_samurai_only_respect_strength:_a_leader_who_takes_what_he_wants_when_he_wants_it._But_I_think_that_he_misreads_the_spirit_of_the_people--we_admire_a_resolute_leader,_but_even_more_a_just_one._We_know_that_a_man_who_does_not_respect_his_own_family's_honor_will_not_respect_the_honor_of_his_followers.
str_nord_rebellion_pretender_story_3 So_I_remain_in_exile_--_except_now_I_am_no_longer_chanting_sutras,_but_practicing_the_ways_of_the_sword_and_bow._If_Lord_Mori_doubts_my_resolve_to_restore_my_birthright,_then_let_him_say_so_face_to_face,_as_we_stare_at_each_other_over_our_blades.
str_rhodok_rebellion_pretender_story_3 Many_of_the_hereditary_vassals_and_I_agreed_that_he_was_too_deep_under_the_influence_of_the_Shinano_retainers._He_even_split_the_inheritance_of_his_domain_for_the_sake_of_my_little_brother,_a_grandson_of_Suwa_Yorishige._In_the_name_of_the_Kai_samurai,_I_had_to_overthrow_him._But_I_failed_the_first_time,_and_now_I'm_here.
str_sarranid_rebellion_pretender_story_3 Alas,_only_my_household_servants_stayed_loyal_to_the_end._But_that_was_all_I_needed._I_possess_nothing_that_they_could_not_carry_out_of_Sunpu_castle_themselves,_but_I_do_own_my_name,_my_honor,_and_my_determination._We_will_soon_see_if_that_is_enough.
str_swadian_rebellion_monarch_response_1 The_princess_thinks_she_should_be_the_head_of_the_Uesugi?_Well,_her_father_had_a_kind_heart,_and_doted_on_his_daughter,_but_a_good-hearted_lord_who_doesn't_use_his_head_can_be_a_curse_to_his_people._And_that's_what_Norimasa_was_--_He_came_running_to_me_after_his_debacle_at_Kawagoe_castle._I_can't_in_good_conscience_serve_a_lord_that_could_lose_so_soundly_when_he_outnumbered_the_enemy_10_to_1.
str_vaegir_rebellion_monarch_response_1 Were_Ashina_to_come_to_me_in_peace,_I_would_honor_him,_and_he_would_become_the_greatest_of_my_vassals._But_as_he_comes_in_war,_I_will_drag_him_before_me_in_chains_and_make_him_acknowledge_my_power,_then_sever_his_head_from_his_neck_so_that_he_cannot_recant.
str_khergit_rebellion_monarch_response_1 My_nephew_Saito_has_perhaps_told_you_of_his_insistence_upon_returning_to_Gifu,_as_though_it_would_not_be_a_thorn_in_my_backside_--_an_unbearable_salient_in_the_heart_of_my_territories._Let_me_tell_you_something._Ever_since_warlords_established_themselves_in_Japan_at_the_expense_of_the_capital,_this_land_has_been_divided._I_intend_to_bring_every_province_under_my_banner_and_reintroduce_peace_and_stability,_like_the_Kamakura_and_Ashikaga_shoguns_before_me.
str_nord_rebellion_monarch_response_1 The_last_Ouchi?_There's_no_such_person_--_they_all_died_in_battle,_I'm_sure_of_it._If_they_sent_a_son_away_to_live_in_a_temple,_he_must_not_have_been_worth_much_at_all._They_probably_kicked_him_out_of_the_clan_--_what_a_pity._I_don't_know_if_one_such_as_that_can_claim_to_be_an_heir_if_he_didn't_even_show_up_to_the_clan's_hour_of_greatest_need!
str_rhodok_rebellion_monarch_response_1 No_doubt_my_son_told_you_that_I'm_a_backstabber_and_maybe_even_a_usurper._Well,_let_me_tell_you_something_--_I_have_decades_of_experience_as_a_warrior,_a_general,_and_ruler._There's_more_to_rulership_than_chauvinism_over_your_birth_province._I_had_to_make_my_fourth_son_the_heir_of_a_significant_portion_of_my_conquered_lands_to_keep_its_inhabitants_pacified._And_for_that,_my_headstrong_first_son_rebelled.
str_sarranid_rebellion_monarch_response_1 The_Imagawa_vassals_knew_what_side_their_bread_was_buttered_on._If_they_hadn't_surrendered_to_me,_they_would_have_been_living_desperate,_hardscrabble_lives._It's_better_this_way,_even_if_their_family_has_been_dispossessed._Her_cousin_--_the_real_heir_to_Imagawa_--_is_the_master_of_tea_ceremonies_at_my_castle,_you_know?
str_swadian_rebellion_monarch_response_2 I_did_her_father_a_favor_by_having_myself_adopted._If_he_had_died_and_left_everything_to_her,_there_would_no_longer_be_an_Uesugi_family.
str_vaegir_rebellion_monarch_response_2 The_Ashina_clan_may_have_dominated_the_Date_for_centuries,_but_we_live_in_an_age_of_war_and_upheaval._I_am_sorry_that_he_felt_that_he_should_coast_on_the_accomplishments_of_his_ancestors,_rather_than_make_a_name_for_himself_as_other_sengoku_daimyo_have._It_is_not_just_heritage_that_makes_one_great_--_I_am_lord_by_support_of_my_vassals,_and_by_right_of_being_the_strongest._That_counts_for_more_than_ancestry,_and_woe_to_any_man_in_this_land_who_says_otherwise.
str_khergit_rebellion_monarch_response_2 Saito_would_call_me_an_upstart_--_a_mere_vice-shugo_of_Owari._Does_he_forget_where_HE_comes_from?_His_grandfather_--_who_named_me_his_heir,_by_the_way_--_was_a_Kyoto_oil_merchant_that_outsmarted_everyone_around_him._I_was_that_old_snake's_protoge_the_Saito's_own_father_wasn't_--_hence_why_I_was_named_his_heir._I_can_tell_you_this_much_about_Saito_--_he_would_make_a_fine_court_nobleman.
str_nord_rebellion_monarch_response_2 Whatever_I_may_or_may_not_have_done_to_secure_my_domain_does_not_matter._I_have_it,_and_that_is_final._If_rulership_was_based_on_family_descent_instead_of_merit,_there_would_be_chaos_and_incompetence_rife_at_every_level._Why_do_you_think_these_wars_are_happening?_Once_the_mighty_have_sorted_things_out_--_whether_from_among_the_masters_or_the_servants,_it_doesn't_matter_--_the_land_will_be_at_peace_again.
str_rhodok_rebellion_monarch_response_2 If_the_little_brat_can_take_me_down,_then_he_deserves_to_have_the_lordship_and_I_will_watch_him_rule_proudly,_from_heaven._But_if_he_can't,_I_will_not_regret_killing_him.
str_sarranid_rebellion_monarch_response_2 I_don't_care_that_she's_running_around_talking_about_her_family_glory._What_can_she_do_without_an_army?_But_in_the_impossible_chance_that_her_words_turn_into_action,_I_won't_go_easy_on_her_just_because_she's_a_woman.

str_feast_lengthy_description_1 The_food_you_provided_was_insufficient_for_your_guests_and_their_retinues,_forcing_them_to_purchase_their_sustenance_from_the_surrounding_countryside_at_grossly_inflated_prices._The_consensus_among_those_who_attended_was_that_you_failed_to_do_your_duty_as_a_host,_diminishing_both_their_trust_in_you_and_your_overall_reputation.
str_feast_lengthy_description_2 The_food_and_drink_you_provided_eventually_ran_out,_forcing_some_guests_to_either_buy_their_own_from_passing_peddlars,_or_send_some_of_their_retinue_home_early._The_more_charitable_attributed_the_shortfall_to_poor_planning_rather_than_meanness,_but_either_way,_it_did_your_reputation_no_good.
str_feast_lengthy_description_3 The_food_and_drink_you_provided_was_adequate_for_your_noble_guests,_although_some_of_the_commoners_in_their_retinues_went_without._You_are_establishing_a_reputation_as_one_who_has_at_least_a_grasp_of_your_social_obligations_as_a_samurai.
str_feast_lengthy_description_4 You_have_provided_enough_food_and_drink,_and_with_sufficient_varieties,_to_do_yourself_credit._The_food,_drink,_and_merriment_have_loosened_your_guests_tongues,_allowing_them_to_converse_candidly_about_the_matters_of_the_domain,_and_deepening_their_trust_in_you.
str_feast_lengthy_description_5 You_have_provided_a_bountiful_table_not_just_for_your_noble_guests_but_for_their_retinues,_with_food_left_over_to_be_distributed_to_the_poor._Your_guests_lavish_praise_upon_you_for_your_generosity,_and_for_your_understanding_of_the_social_obligations_of_your_rank._The_conversation,_fueled_by_the_food_and_drink,_has_been_merry,_strengthening_the_bonds_between_those_who_attended.
str_feast_lengthy_description_6 The_domain_will_be_speaking_of_the_bounty_of_your_table_for_months_to_come,_and_it_will_become_the_standard_to_which_all_other_feasts_will_aspire._You_have_filled_the_bellies_not_just_of_your_noble_guests_and_their_retinues,_but_also_of_the_poor_who_flocked_to_the_gates._

str_quick_battle_troop_3 The_second_son_of_a_minor_noble_living_near_Uxkhal,_Hegen_was_educated_in_the_art_of_war_and_single_combat._After_being_knighted_he_served_as_a_paid_knight_in_the_army_of_the_lord_of_Uxkhal_and_fought_against_the_Vaegirs_before_leading_a_group_of_outriders_that_defeated_a_Khergit_raid_near_Amere._The_ensuing_counter_raid_and_the_following_two_campaigns_earned_him_glory_and_fame_as_a_warrior._Unfortunately,_he_lost_any_chance_of_further_prestige_when_peace_was_declared_and_he_was_discharged._With_no_hope_of_inheriting_and_his_skills_at_war_languishing_in_peace,_he_assembled_other_young_warriors_and_set_out_as_a_mercenary_captain._He_now_hopes_to_take_advantage_of_the_fact_that_Japan_never_lacks_warring_states_in_need_of_mercenaries.
str_quick_battle_troop_4 Konrad_is_a_professional_mercenary_from_the_distant_land_of_Balion,_far_beyond_the_vast_western_ocean._Having_spent_most_of_his_years_on_campaign_and_seen_countless_battles,_Konrad_has_grown_to_love_his_life_as_a_soldier_of_fortune._Though_he_once_had_his_nose_flattened_by_a_mace_blow_and_has_received_many_wounds,_he_has_nevertheless_survived_this_harsh_existence_through_the_strength_of_his_arm,_innate_cunning_and_pure_luck._Hearing_of_the_lucrative_career_opportunities_awaiting_a_man_of_his_talents_in_Japan,_Konrad_chartered_a_vessel_and_crossed_the_sea_with_his_men_in_search_of_new_wars_to_fight_in._A_sellsword_with_no_ties_to_any_of_the_Japan_domains,_he_is_more_than_happy_to_offer_his_services_to_any_lord_with_a_fat_enough_coin-purse.
str_quick_battle_troop_5 Sverre_is_one_of_the_so-called_sea_raiders_--_freebooters_and_lawless_men_from_the_icy_realm_of_Jumne_beyond_the_North_Sea,_also_said_to_be_the_ancestral_home_of_the_Nords._Already_as_a_young_man_he_has_been_along_on_many_raids_against_both_his_distant_cousins_in_the_Wercheg_region_and_the_Vaegirs._However,_Sverre_was_always_a_sharp_lad,_and_it_didn't_take_him_long_to_see_that_Japan_was_a_far_more_prosperous_land_than_his_own,_and_that_he_could_have_a_better_life_here_than_among_his_own_people._During_a_raid_on_Jayek,_Sverre_stole_away_while_his_comrades_were_busy_looting_the_village_and_taking_captives._Passing_himself_off_as_a_yokel_from_the_Chalbek_mountains,_Sverre_quickly_built_up_a_reputation_for_himself_as_a_fierce_fighter,_and_he_now_seeks_his_fortune_at_the_head_of_a_mercenary_band.
str_quick_battle_troop_6 Hailing_from_Charnye,_in_the_far_reaches_of_the_Vaegir_tundra,_Borislav_is_a_hunter._For_all_of_his_life_he_has_tracked_the_beasts_of_the_wild_for_their_meat_and_fur,_living_off_the_land_just_as_his_forefathers_had_done_in_happier_days,_before_the_endless_wars._Now,_the_game_is_quick_to_take_fright_from_the_constant_sounds_of_battle,_and_the_wanton_slaughter_of_animals_by_soldiers_has_left_empty_those_forests_that_have_not_been_burnt_down._Facing_starvation,_Borislav_chose_to_turn_his_great_skill_with_bow_and_spear,_learned_from_hunting_stag,_wolf,_and_bear,_to_the_practice_of_hunting_men,_and_his_steady_hand_and_keen_eye_have_claimed_many_lives._Borislav_does_not_care_much_for_the_disputes_of_kingdoms,_and_is_only_really_interested_in_keeping_himself_and_his_men_fed.
str_quick_battle_troop_7 Stavros_was_born_in_the_independent_city-state_of_Zendar,_and_spent_much_of_his_adult_life_serving_in_the_town_watch_under_the_famous_constable_Hareck._Stavros'_leadership_and_prowess_were_instrumental_in_ridding_the_area_of_the_dreaded_river_pirates,_but_even_he_was_powerless_against_the_calamity_that_befell_the_city._When_Zendar_was_razed_to_the_ground_by_a_great_horde_of_sea_raiders,_Stavros_fled_the_burning_city_in_a_crowd_of_refugees._After_a_brief_period_of_wandering_and_odd_jobs,_he_found_a_place_in_a_mercenary_company,_eventually_rising_to_become_its_leader_due_to_his_dedication_and_tactical_aptitude._He_now_devotes_most_of_his_efforts_to_working_with_manhunters_and_local_authorities_against_the_sea_raiders_and_other_outlaws,_trying_to_keep_the_land_safe_for_travelers.
str_quick_battle_troop_8 Growing_up_with_one_of_the_nomadic_tribes_deep_in_the_desert_beyond_Sarranid_lands,_Gamara_learned_early_on_how_to_hunt_with_sling_and_spear._However,_the_simple_life_and_pitiless_conditions_in_the_desert_did_not_satisfy_her,_and_she_burned_with_a_desire_to_see_the_great_world_beyond_that_she_had_heard_so_many_wondrous_tales_about._Life_is_not_easy_for_an_adventuring_young_woman,_and_Gamara_had_to_learn_the_ways_of_Japan_quickly._Taking_the_weapons_and_armor_of_a_soldier_who_had_attacked_her_after_a_dispute,_Gamara_now_hides_her_beauty_under_thick_Sarranid_garb,_and_many_never_even_suspect_she_is_a_woman_-_certainly_as_a_force_on_the_battlefield_she_is_as_dangerous_as_any_man._She_has_gathered_about_her_a_group_of_followers,_and_together_they_wander_the_war-torn_land_in_search_of_glory.
str_quick_battle_troop_9 Aethrod_is_not_a_noble_person._He's_changed_his_name_twice,_and_is_blamed_for_most_of_the_crimes_on_Vaegir_territory._True_or_not,_he_claims_to_never_have_taken_an_innocent_man's_life,_and_considers_himself_a_patriotic_citizen,_several_times_bringing_his_band_or_renegades_to_the_assistance_of_his_faction,_when_it_is_threatened._In_times_of_peace,_however,_most_lords_must_be_careful_when_he_is_in_the_vicinity_due_to_his_daring_personality_and_willingness_to_challenge_a_lord._Born_and_rasied_in_the_slums_of_Reyvadin,_he_learned_how_to_use_a_bow_at_an_early_age_and_ran_away_from_home_a_fourteen._Now_at_thirty_two,_his_archery_skills_are_near_perfect_and_though_he_can't_ride_a_horse_well,_he_can_hit_one_at_the_furthest_of_distances._Tough_as_nails_and_sharp_as_a_hawk,_he_is_a_true_local_legend.
str_quick_battle_troop_10 Being_the_daughter_of_one_of_the_most_infamous_bandit_leaders_in_the_Sarranid_realm_isn't_always_easy,_but_Zaira_seems_to_have_managed_quite_well._Unlike_most_women_she_grew_up_learning_the_ways_of_the_desert_warrior_and_is_deadly_with_the_sword_as_well_as_the_bow._While_the_other_girls_her_age_learned_how_to_manage_the_household,_Zaira_learned_how_to_best_gut_a_merchant_before_taking_his_money._At_the_age_of_sixteen_Zaira_had_killed_more_men_than_the_average_veteran_in_the_Sultan's_army._Just_before_her_twentieth_brithday_her_father_was_killed_in_brawl_with_another_bandit_leader._As_the_only_child,_Zaira_now_took_control_of_her_father's_band._After_avenging_her_father,_she_quickly_picked_up_where_he_had_left._Now_she's_on_a_good_way_of_establishing_her_own_reputation_has_a_bandit_leader.
str_quick_battle_troop_11 Argo_Sendnar_had_quite_a_diversified_life._When_he_arrived_at_Japan,_working_as_a_trader,_he_hoped_for_more_income_than_in_Lokti._Little_did_he_know,_that_the_wartorn_Japan_was_a_wasps'_nest_for_bandits_and_cutthroats_that_made_trading_a_lot_more_complicated_than_in_Lokti._Being_bought_out_by_another_competeting_trader,_after_losing_all_his_goods_and_money_due_to_caravan_raids,_he_was_forced_to_serve_as_a_caravan_guard_to_make_a_living._Despite_his_pathetic_fighting_skills,_he_soon_found_an_employment_on_one_of_the_more_dangerous_routes_through_Japan._Due_to_sheer_luck_he_managed_to_stay_alive_long_enough_to_aquire_enough_combat_experience_and_money_to_start_his_own_buisness_as_a_caravan_master,_offering_his_services_to_traders_in_need_of_defense_for_their_goods.
